/* CGNV$CLOSE_ALL_WINDOWS */
/* Close any open windows in the form */
BEGIN
  CGNV$.nav_enter_query := FALSE;
  IF (name_in('SYSTEM.MODE') = 'ENTER-QUERY') THEN
    exit_form;
  ELSE
    CGNV$.CLOSE_ALL_WINDOWS(name_in('SYSTEM.FORM_STATUS'));
  END IF;
END;

/* CGYR$SET_DATE_FORMAT */
/* Establish Single Standard Format Mask with 4-digit-year element */
BEGIN
  set_application_property(DATE_FORMAT_COMPATIBILITY_MODE, '5.0');
  set_application_property(PLSQL_DATE_FORMAT, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS');
  set_application_property(BUILTIN_DATE_FORMAT, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS');
  forms_ddl('ALTER SESSION SET NLS_DATE_FORMAT = ''YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS''');
END;

/* CGNV$PRE_FORM_NAVCCF */
/* Set if we want to close child forms as well as child windows */
  DECLARE
  rg_id RECORDGROUP;
  gc_type GROUPCOLUMN;
  gc_name GROUPCOLUMN;
  gc_parent GROUPCOLUMN;
  gc_tag GROUPCOLUMN;
  gc_extra GROUPCOLUMN;
BEGIN
  CGNV$.nav_opening_wnd := FALSE;
  :global.CGNV_last_closed_form := '0';
  :global.CGNV_child_form := find_form(get_application_property(FORM_NAME)).id;
  rg_id := create_group('CGSH$FORM_OBJECTS');
  gc_type := add_group_column(rg_id, 'OBJECT_TYPE', CHAR_COLUMN, 2);
  gc_name := add_group_column(rg_id, 'OBJECT_NAME', CHAR_COLUMN, 40);
  gc_parent := add_group_column(rg_id, 'PARENT_NAME', CHAR_COLUMN, 40);
  gc_tag := add_group_column(rg_id, 'ITEM_TAG', CHAR_COLUMN, 40);
  gc_extra := add_group_column(rg_id, 'EXTRA_TEXT', CHAR_COLUMN, 240);
  add_group_row(rg_id, 1);
  set_group_char_cell(gc_type, 1, 'WN');
  set_group_char_cell(gc_name, 1, 'DATE_LOV_WINDOW');
  set_group_char_cell(gc_parent, 1, '');
  add_group_row(rg_id, 2);
  set_group_char_cell(gc_type, 2, 'WN');
  set_group_char_cell(gc_name, 2, 'WINDOW');
  set_group_char_cell(gc_parent, 2, '');
END;

/* CGGN$GET_DATE_AND_USER */
/* Get the current user and date; store in items for general use */
BEGIN
  DECLARE
    CURSOR C IS
      SELECT  SYSDATE, USER
      FROM    SYS.DUAL;
  BEGIN
    OPEN C;
    FETCH C
    INTO    :PARAMETER.CGU$SYSDATE, :PARAMETER.CGU$USER;
    IF C%NOTFOUND THEN
      CLOSE C;
      MESSAGE('Internal Error: No row in table SYS.DUAL');
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
    END IF;
    CLOSE C;
  END;
END;

DECLARE
   vPort WB_WAYBILL_HDR.origin%type;
   vSuperRole Varchar2(12);
BEGIN
   BEGIN
      select 1 into vSuperRole
      from   user_role_privs 
      where  granted_role like 'WBS_SUPER_USER' 
      and    rownum < 2;
   exception
      when others then vSuperRole := '0';
   END;

   if vSuperRole = '1' then
      -- set_block_property('WB_WAYBILL_HDR', DEFAULT_WHERE, '');
      null;
   else
      begin
         select port_code
         into   vPort
         from   wb_employees
         where  code = user;
      exception
      	 when no_data_found then 
            vPort := '-1111';
            msg_alert ('No Port/Location assigned to you. Please contact your supervisor.', 'W', FALSE);
      end;
      -- set_block_property('WB_WAYBILL_HDR', DEFAULT_WHERE, 'origin=''' || vPort || '''');
   end if;

   -- msg_alert ('check default where: ' || get_block_property('WB_WAYBILL_HDR', DEFAULT_WHERE), 'I', FALSE);
END;

/*CGAP$TES_SEQUENCE_BEFORE*/
DECLARE
   v_current_block_name  pkg_mylib_form_types. subtyp_obj_name;
   c_last_block_name  CONSTANT v_current_block_name% TYPE :=
      Get_Form_Property ( :system.current_form, last_block );

   v_current_item_name  pkg_mylib_form_types. subtyp_obj_name;
   v_current_item_id  ITEM;
   v_last_item_name  v_current_item_name% TYPE;

BEGIN

   v_current_block_name :=
      Get_Form_Property ( :system.current_form, first_block );
   << Loop_All_Blocks >>
   LOOP
      IF Get_Block_Property ( v_current_block_name, records_displayed ) > 1
      THEN

         v_last_item_name :=
            Get_Block_Property ( v_current_block_name, last_item );

         v_current_item_name :=
            Get_Block_Property ( v_current_block_name, first_item );
         << Loop_All_Block_Items >>
         LOOP
         	  v_current_item_id :=
         	     Find_Item
            	    ( v_current_block_name || '.' || v_current_item_name );

            IF Get_Item_Property
            	    ( v_current_item_id, displayed ) = 'TRUE' AND
             	 Get_Item_Property
            	    ( v_current_item_id, item_canvas ) IS NOT NULL AND
            	 Get_Item_Property
            	    ( v_current_item_id,
                    records_displayed ) > 1 -- displayed > once; this property is NEVER 0 at runtime;
            THEN
               Set_Item_Property
                  ( v_current_item_id,
                    current_record_attribute,
                    'CG$CURRENT_RECORD' ); -- "safe" to hard-code name bec this is a STD visual attr.;
            END IF;

         EXIT WHEN v_current_item_name = v_last_item_name;
            v_current_item_name :=
               Get_Item_Property ( v_current_item_id, nextitem );

         END LOOP Loop_All_Block_Items;

      END IF;

   EXIT WHEN v_current_block_name = c_last_block_name;
      v_current_block_name :=
         Get_Block_Property ( v_current_block_name, nextblock );

   END LOOP Loop_All_Blocks;
END;

/* CGLY$COPY_USER_DATE */
/* Values from USER and DATE items on content canvas 0 in the control */
/* block will be \"fired\" to all other USER and DATE items           */
/* on other content canvas.                                           */
BEGIN
  CGBS2$.SET_COORD_STYLE( 'P' );
  CGBS2$.SET_QRY_ON_ENTRY( 'Y' );
  CGBS2$.SET_NAV_FROM_BLOCK( 'WB_WAYBILL_DTL' );
  :CG$CTRL.CG$DT := :PARAMETER.CGU$SYSDATE;
  copy(name_in('PARAMETER.CGU$USER'), 'CG$CTRL.CG$US');
END;

/* CGBS$KEY_EXEQRY_FRM */
/* Check if query is allowed to avoid unnecessary coordination */
BEGIN

    MESSAGE('Error: Query not allowed in this block');
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
  END IF;
  CGBS$.DO_KEYQRY( name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK'), 'EXECUTE_QUERY', name_in('SYSTEM.MODE'));
END;

/* CGBS$KEY_CLRBLK_FRM */
/* Perform checks prior to clearing block */
BEGIN
  IF ( CGBS2$.IS_RECORD_DIRTY(name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK')) ) THEN
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
  END IF;
  IF (name_in('SYSTEM.BLOCK_STATUS') = 'CHANGED' OR CGBS2$.IS_COMMIT_NEEDED( name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK') ) ) THEN
    CGBS2$.DO_COMMIT_DIALOGUE;
  END IF;
  clear_block( NO_VALIDATE );
END;
   - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                        Yes
   - Execution Hierarchy                             Override
   * Display in 'Keyboard Help'                      Yes
   - 'Keyboard Help' Text                            
   - Trigger Steps                                   
   ----------
   * Name                                            KEY-CLRREC
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   - Trigger Style                                   PL/SQL
   * Trigger Text                                    

/* CGBS$KEY_CLRREC */
/* Avoid clearing details if current row is new and invalid */
BEGIN
  IF ( CGBS2$.IS_RECORD_DIRTY(name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK')) ) THEN
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
  END IF;
  IF ( CGBS2$.IS_COMMIT_NEEDED( name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK') ) ) THEN
    CGBS2$.DO_COMMIT_DIALOGUE;
  END IF;
  clear_record;
END;

/* CGBS$TOGGLE_QUERY_MODE */
/* This changes the mode of block synchronization so that if it is */
/* currently ON, then it is changed to OFF, and vice-versa.        */
/* It also queries the dependent blocks as appropriate for the     */
/* new mode.                                                       */
BEGIN
  CGBS$TOGGLE( :GLOBAL.CG$QUERY_MODE );
END;

/* CGWH$SET_AUDIT_UPD_FLDS */
/* Set the date and/or user updated items to the system date/oracle user */
BEGIN
   IF :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.wgt = 0 THEN
      msg_alert('System does not accept zero value for ''Kgs''. Please enter value for Kilogram.', 'E', TRUE);
   END IF;

   copy(SYSDATE, 'WB_WAYBILL_DTL.PRICED_DT');
   copy(name_in('PARAMETER.CGU$USER'), 'WB_WAYBILL_DTL.PRICED_BY');
END;


     - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                      Yes
     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override

/* CGTE$BLK_LEVEL_ERROR_TRAP */
/* Trap errors returning from the server and report in a user friendly manner */
BEGIN
  BEGIN
    CGTE$WB_WAYBILL_DTL_ERRORS;
  EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
      CGTE$OTHER_EXCEPTIONS;
  END;
END;
     - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                      Yes
     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override
     * Display in 'Keyboard Help'                    Yes
     - 'Keyboard Help' Text                          
     - Trigger Steps                                 
     ----------
     * Name                                          POST-QUERY
     - Subclass Information                          
     - Comments                                      
     - Trigger Style                                 PL/SQL
     * Trigger Text                                  

begin
   select reference_no, waybill_date, origin, destination, 
          shipper, shipper_name, consignee, consignee_name, 
          service_mode, payment_mode, status, payment_status, 
          special_instructions, created_by, checked_by,
          dt_created, checked_dt
   into   :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_pro_forma, :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_waybill_date, :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_origin, :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_destination, 
          :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_shipper, :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_shipper_name, :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_consignee, :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_consignee_name,
          :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_service_mode, :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_payment_mode, :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_status, :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_payment_status,
          :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_special, :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_prepared_by, :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_checked_by,
          :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_prepared_dt, :wb_waybill_dtl.wahd_checked_dt
   from   wb_waybill_hdr
   where  waybill_no = :wb_waybill_dtl.waybill_no;
exception
	 when no_data_found then null;
end;

begin
   select description
   into   :wb_waybill_dtl.comm_name
   from   wb_commodities
   where  code =  :wb_waybill_dtl.comm_code;
exception
	 when no_data_found then null;
end;

begin
   select loading_no, container_code, voyage_no
	 into   :wb_waybill_dtl.loading_no, :wb_waybill_dtl.container_code, :wb_waybill_dtl.voyage_no
   from (
	 select loading_no, container_code, voyage_no
	 from   wb_container_waybill
	 where  waybill_no = :wb_waybill_dtl.waybill_no
	 order  by dt_created )
	 where  rownum = 1;
exception
   when no_data_found then null;
end;

declare
  vDefWhere Varchar2(2000);
begin
  vDefWhere := 'exists (select 1 from wb_waybill_hdr where wb_waybill_hdr.waybill_no = wb_waybill_dtl.waybill_no and wb_waybill_hdr.status = ''AC'')';
  set_block_property('WB_WAYBILL_DTL', default_where, vDefWhere); 
end;


     - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                      Yes
     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override
     - Display in 'Keyboard Help'                    No
     - 'Keyboard Help' Text                          
     - Trigger Steps                                 
     ----------
     * Name                                          KEY-DELREC
     - Subclass Information                          
     - Comments                                      
     - Trigger Style                                 PL/SQL
     * Trigger Text                                  

begin
   :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.QTY := 0;
   :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.CBM := 0;
   :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WGT := 0;
   :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.DECLARED_VALUE := 0;
   delete_record;
end;

     - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                      Yes
     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override
     - Display in 'Keyboard Help'                    No
     - 'Keyboard Help' Text                          
     - Trigger Steps                                 
     ----------
     * Name                                          POST-UPDATE
     - Subclass Information                          
     - Comments                                      
     - Trigger Style                                 PL/SQL
     * Trigger Text                                  

declare
   nAmt Number;
   nVal Number;
   nCbm Number;
   nWgt Number;
   nQty Number;
begin
   select sum(qty), sum(wgt), sum(cbm), sum(total_amt), sum(valuation_amt)
   into   nQty, nWgt, nCbm, nAmt, nVal
   from   wb_waybill_dtl
   where  waybill_no = :wb_waybill_dtl.waybill_no;

   update wb_waybill_hdr
   set    total_amt       = nAmt,
          total_valuation = nVal,
          total_cbm       = nCbm,
          total_wgt       = nWgt,
          total_qty       = nQty,
          priced_by       = user,
          priced_dt       = sysdate
   where  waybill_no = :wb_waybill_dtl.waybill_no;
end;

     - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                      Yes
     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override
     - Display in 'Keyboard Help'                    No
     - 'Keyboard Help' Text                          
     - Trigger Steps                                 
     ----------
     * Name                                          PRE-QUERY
     - Subclass Information                          
     - Comments                                      
     - Trigger Style                                 PL/SQL
     * Trigger Text                                  

declare
   vDefWhere varchar2(4000);
   vWhere    varchar2(4000);
begin
   vDefWhere := get_block_property('WB_WAYBILL_DTL', default_where);
   if :wb_waybill_dtl.loading_no is not null then
      if vWhere is null then
         vWhere := ' exists (select 1 from wb_container_waybill cowa where cowa.waybill_no = wb_waybill_dtl.waybill_no and cowa.loading_no = ' || :wb_waybill_dtl.loading_no || ')';
      else
         vWhere := vWhere || ' and exists (select 1 from wb_container_waybill cowa where cowa.waybill_no = wb_waybill_dtl.waybill_no and cowa.loading_no = ' || :wb_waybill_dtl.loading_no || ')';
      end if;
   end if;
   if :wb_waybill_dtl.container_code is not null then
      if vWhere is null then
         vWhere := ' exists (select 1 from wb_container_waybill cowa where cowa.waybill_no = wb_waybill_dtl.waybill_no and cowa.container_code like ''' || :wb_waybill_dtl.container_code  || ''')';
      else
         vWhere := vWhere || ' and exists (select 1 from wb_container_waybill cowa where cowa.waybill_no = wb_waybill_dtl.waybill_no and cowa.container_code like ''' || :wb_waybill_dtl.container_code  || ''')';
      end if;
   end if;
   if :wb_waybill_dtl.voyage_no is not null then
      if vWhere is null then
         vWhere := ' exists (select 1 from wb_container_waybill cowa where cowa.waybill_no = wb_waybill_dtl.waybill_no and cowa.voyage_no like ''' || :wb_waybill_dtl.voyage_no  || ''')';
      else
         vWhere := vWhere || ' and exists (select 1 from wb_container_waybill cowa where cowa.waybill_no = wb_waybill_dtl.waybill_no and cowa.voyage_no like ''' || :wb_waybill_dtl.voyage_no  || ''')';
      end if;
   end if;
   if vWhere is not null then
      if vDefWhere is null then
         vWhere := 'where ' || vWhere ;
      else
         vWhere := vDefWhere || ' and ' || vWhere ;
      end if;
   else
      vWhere := vDefWhere;
   end if;
   -- msg_alert ('check vWhere: ' || vWhere , 'I', FALSE);
   set_block_property('WB_WAYBILL_DTL', default_where, vWhere);
end;

declare
	 nCnt Number:=0;
begin
   if :wb_waybill_dtl.description is not null then
      for i in (select tariff, rate, uome, comm_code, class_type from wb_waybill_dtl where description like :wb_waybill_dtl.description || '%' order by dt_created desc) loop
          :wb_waybill_dtl.uome   := i.uome;
          :wb_waybill_dtl.tariff := i.tariff;
          :wb_waybill_dtl.rate   := i.rate;
          if :wb_waybill_dtl.comm_code is null then
             :wb_waybill_dtl.comm_code := i.comm_code;
          end if;
          if :wb_waybill_dtl.class_type is null then
             :wb_waybill_dtl.class_type := i.class_type;
          end if;
          exit;
      end loop;
   end if;
end;

declare
   nRetr Number(3);
   vDescription wb_waybill_dtl.description%type;
   vClass       wb_waybill_dtl.class_type%type;
begin
   select upper(description), class_code 
   into   vDescription, vClass
   from   wb_commodities
   where  code = :wb_waybill_dtl.comm_code;
   
   if :wb_waybill_dtl.description is null then
      :wb_waybill_dtl.description := :wb_waybill_dtl.comm_name;
   --elsif :wb_waybill_dtl.description <> vDescription then
   --   :wb_waybill_dtl.description := vDescription;
   end if;

   :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.CLASS_TYPE := vClass;
   IF :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_PAYMENT_MODE in ('AO', 'PO') THEN
      sp_get_lcl_rate(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_WAYBILL_DATE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_SHIPPER, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.CLASS_TYPE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_ORIGIN, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_DESTINATION, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.COMM_CODE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_SERVICE_MODE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.BASIS, nRetr, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.TARIFF);
   ELSE
      sp_get_lcl_rate(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_WAYBILL_DATE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_CONSIGNEE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.CLASS_TYPE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_ORIGIN, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_DESTINATION, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.COMM_CODE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_SERVICE_MODE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.BASIS, nRetr, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.TARIFF);
   END IF;
   :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.RATE   := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.TARIFF;
exception
   when no_data_found then
      msg_alert('Commodity code does not exists. Please select Commodity.', 'E', TRUE);
end;

       - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                    Yes
       - Execution Hierarchy                         Override
       - Display in 'Keyboard Help'                  No
       - 'Keyboard Help' Text                        
       - Trigger Steps

     * Name                                          COMM_NAME
     * Item Type                                     Display Item

begin
   if :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.RATE > 0 and :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.QTY > 0 and :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.BASIS = 'QTY' then
       :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.QTY * :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.RATE;
   end if;
	 :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.TOTAL_AMT := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT + :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT;
   check_valuation;
end;

declare
	 nCnt Number:=0;
   err_txt VARCHAR2(80) := 'Are you sure you want to enter new Unit of Measure?'; 
   al_id ALERT; 
   al_button Number; 
begin
   al_id := FIND_ALERT('CFG_2BUTTON'); 
   SET_ALERT_PROPERTY(al_id, alert_message_text, err_txt ); 

   select count(1)
   into   nCnt
   from   wb_unit_of_measures
   where  uome = :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.UOME;

   if nCnt = 0 then
      al_button := SHOW_ALERT( al_id ); 
      if al_button = 89 then
         :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.UOME := null;
         msg_alert('Please press F9 to view list of Unit of Measure.', 'I', TRUE);
      end if;
   end if;
end;

   ELSIF :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_PAYMENT_MODE = 'AO' then
      :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT := sf_get_valuation(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_WAYBILL_DATE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_SHIPPER_VALUATION, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.DECLARED_VALUE);

   END IF;

	 :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.TOTAL_AMT := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT + :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT;

declare
   nRetr Number(3);
begin
   if :wb_waybill_dtl.description is null then
      :wb_waybill_dtl.description := :wb_waybill_dtl.comm_name;
   end if;

   IF :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_PAYMENT_MODE in ('AO', 'PO') THEN
      sp_get_lcl_rate(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_WAYBILL_DATE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_SHIPPER, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.CLASS_TYPE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_ORIGIN, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_DESTINATION, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.COMM_CODE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_SERVICE_MODE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.BASIS, nRetr, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.TARIFF);
   ELSE
      sp_get_lcl_rate(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_WAYBILL_DATE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_CONSIGNEE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.CLASS_TYPE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_ORIGIN, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_DESTINATION, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.COMM_CODE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_SERVICE_MODE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.BASIS, nRetr, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.TARIFF);
   END IF;
   :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.RATE   := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.TARIFF;

   if nRetr = -1 and :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.RATE = 0 then
      msg_alert ('No rates available for this customer/class type/origin/destination/basis and No Standard rate available.', 'I', FALSE);
   elsif nRetr = -1 then
      msg_alert ('No rates available for this customer/class type/origin/destination/basis, Standard rate applied.', 'I', FALSE);
   end if;

 	 if :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.BASIS = 'QTY' then
	 	  :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.QTY * :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.RATE;
 	 elsif :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.BASIS = 'KGS' then
	 	  :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WGT * :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.RATE;
	 else
	 	  :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.CBM * :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.RATE;
	 end if;
	 :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.TOTAL_AMT := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT + :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT;
   check_valuation;
end;

       - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                    Yes
       - Execution Hierarchy                         Override
       - Display in 'Keyboard Help'                  No
       - 'Keyboard Help' Text                        
       - Trigger Steps                               
       ----------
     ----------
     * Name                                          TARIFF
     - Item Type                                     Text Item
     - Subclass Information                          
     * Comments                                      *******************************************************************

       * Trigger Text                                

begin
 	 if :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.BASIS = 'QTY' then
	 	  :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.QTY * :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.RATE;
 	 elsif :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.BASIS = 'KGS' then
	 	  :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WGT * :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.RATE;
	 else
	 	  :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.CBM * :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.RATE;
	 end if;
	 :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.TOTAL_AMT := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT + :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT;
   check_valuation;
end;

/* CGLY$WHEN_BUTTON_PRESSED */
/* Replicate default menu functionality */
DECLARE
  vStatus Varchar2(16);
	pl_id   ParamList;
	pl_name VARCHAR2(10) := 'tempdata';
  vDefWhere Varchar2(2048);
BEGIN
   if :wb_waybill_dtl.item_no is null then
      msg_alert ('Please select Commodity!', 'E', TRUE);
   end if;
   pl_id := Get_Parameter_List(pl_name);
   IF NOT Id_Null(pl_id) THEN
      Destroy_Parameter_List(pl_id);
	 END IF;
   pl_id := Create_Parameter_List(pl_name);
   IF Id_Null(pl_id) THEN
      Message('Error creating parameter list '||pl_name);
	    RAISE Form_Trigger_Failure;
   END IF;

   Add_Parameter(pl_id,'cg$waybill_no',TEXT_PARAMETER, :wb_waybill_dtl.waybill_no);
   Add_Parameter(pl_id,'cg$item_no',TEXT_PARAMETER, :wb_waybill_dtl.item_no);
   call_form('WBST0025.fmx', NO_HIDE, NO_REPLACE, NO_QUERY_ONLY, pl_id);

END;

       * Trigger Text                                

declare
	 vWaybillNo Varchar2(40);
begin
   vWaybillNo := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAYBILL_NO;

   IF :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT = 0 and :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.DECLARED_VALUE > 0 THEN
      IF :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_PAYMENT_MODE = 'AD' then
         :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT := sf_get_valuation(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_WAYBILL_DATE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_CONSIGNEE_VALUATION, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.DECLARED_VALUE);
      ELSIF :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_PAYMENT_MODE = 'AO' then
         :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT := sf_get_valuation(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_WAYBILL_DATE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_SHIPPER_VALUATION, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.DECLARED_VALUE);
      ELSE
         :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT := sf_get_valuation(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_WAYBILL_DATE, -1, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.DECLARED_VALUE);
      END IF;
	   :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.TOTAL_AMT := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT + :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT;   
   END IF;

   commit;
   sp_recompute_waybill_amt(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAYBILL_NO);
   set_block_property('WB_WAYBILL_DTL', default_where, 'where waybill_no = ''' || vWaybillNo || '''');
   execute_query;
   set_block_property('WB_WAYBILL_DTL', default_where, '');
end;

/*CGAP$TEMPLATE_NAMED_ROUTINE*/
PROCEDURE displayCalendar IS
BEGIN
   if Name_In ( :system.cursor_item ) is null then
      date_lov.get_date (sysdate, :system.cursor_item );
   else
      date_lov.get_date (Name_In ( :system.cursor_item ), :system.cursor_item );
   end if;
END;

      ( Get_View_Property
           ( Get_Item_Property
                ( :system.cursor_item, item_canvas ),
             window_name ),
        Name_In('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_ITEM'),
        Name_In('SYSTEM.FORM_STATUS'),
        FALSE );
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            MSG_ALERT
   - Subclass Information                            
   * Comments                                        CG$IGNORE_ON_DESIGN_CAPTURE
   * Program Unit Text                               

procedure msg_alert(
errm in VARCHAR2,           /* message */
errt in VARCHAR2,           /* message type */
rftf in boolean         /* raise form_trigger_failure ? */
) is      /* message parameters */
/*
* ----------------------------------------------------------------
* CHANGE HISTORY:
* DATE   PERSON      CHANGE
* ------ ----------- ---------------------------------------------
*
*/

alert_is alert;
alert_button number;

BEGIN

     IF (errt = 'F')
     THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_SYSTEM_ERROR');
     ELSIF (errt = 'E')
        THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_ERROR');
        ELSIF (errt = 'W')
           THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_WARNING_A');
              ELSIF (errt = 'I')
                 THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_INFORMATION');
                    ELSIF (errt = '2')
	                	THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_2BUTTON');
				               ELSIF (errt = '3')
        			         THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_3BUTTON');
					                 ELSE MESSAGE(errm);
     end if;

     IF (errt IN ('F','E','W','I'))
     THEN SET_ALERT_PROPERTY(alert_is,ALERT_MESSAGE_TEXT,errm);
          alert_button := SHOW_ALERT(alert_is);
     END IF;

     IF (rftf)
     THEN
       RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
     END IF;


END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGDV$POPULATE_DYNAMIC_LISTS
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGDV$POPULATE_DYNAMIC_LISTS */
PROCEDURE CGDV$POPULATE_DYNAMIC_LISTS IS
/* Read each lists values from its record group and populate the list */
  temp NUMBER;  /* Return value of populate_group call */
  rg_id RECORDGROUP;  /* Return value of populate_group call */
BEGIN
  rg_id := create_group_from_query('CGDV$DLRG',
    'SELECT RV_MEANING, RV_LOW_VALUE '||
    'FROM   CG_REF_CODES '||
    'WHERE  RV_DOMAIN = ''SERVICE_MODE'' '||
    'ORDER BY  1');
  temp := populate_group(rg_id);
  populate_list('WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_SERVICE_MODE', rg_id);
  delete_group(rg_id);

  rg_id := create_group_from_query('CGDV$DLRG',
    'SELECT RV_MEANING, RV_LOW_VALUE '||
    'FROM   CG_REF_CODES '||
    'WHERE  RV_DOMAIN = ''PAYMENT_MODE'' '||
    'ORDER BY  1');
  temp := populate_group(rg_id);
  populate_list('WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_PAYMENT_MODE', rg_id);
  delete_group(rg_id);

  rg_id := create_group_from_query('CGDV$DLRG',
    'SELECT RV_MEANING, RV_LOW_VALUE '||
    'FROM   CG_REF_CODES '||
    'WHERE  RV_DOMAIN = ''PAYMENT_STATUS'' '||
    'ORDER BY  1');
  temp := populate_group(rg_id);
  populate_list('WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_PAYMENT_STATUS', rg_id);
  delete_group(rg_id);

  rg_id := create_group_from_query('CGDV$DLRG',
    'SELECT RV_MEANING, RV_LOW_VALUE '||
    'FROM   CG_REF_CODES '||
    'WHERE  RV_DOMAIN = ''BASIS'' '||
    'ORDER BY  1');
  temp := populate_group(rg_id);
  populate_list('WB_WAYBILL_DTL.BASIS', rg_id);
  delete_group(rg_id);

END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGUV$CHK_WHDR_PK
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGUV$CHK_WHDR_PK */
PROCEDURE CGUV$CHK_WHDR_PK(
   P_WAYBILL_NO IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Item value */
/* Check uniqueness against primary/unique constraint        */
/* Note : NO_DATA_FOUND exception handled by calling trigger */
  CG$DUMMY VARCHAR2(1);
BEGIN
    DECLARE
      CURSOR C IS
        SELECT  '1'
        FROM    WB_WAYBILL_HDR
        WHERE   WAYBILL_NO = P_WAYBILL_NO;
    BEGIN
      OPEN C;
      FETCH C
      INTO    CG$DUMMY;
      IF C%NOTFOUND THEN
        CLOSE C;
        RAISE NO_DATA_FOUND;
      END IF;
      CLOSE C;
    END;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGFK$CHK_WB_WAYBILL_DTL_WDTL_W
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGFK$CHK_WB_WAYBILL_DTL_WDTL_W */
/* Validate foreign key value/query lookup data. */
PROCEDURE CGFK$CHK_WB_WAYBILL_DTL_WDTL_W(
   P_WAYBILL_NO   IN VARCHAR2   /* Value in item :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAYBILL_NO */
)
IS
  CG$DUMMY VARCHAR2(1);

  CURSOR C1 IS
    SELECT 'x'
    FROM   WB_WAYBILL_HDR WB_WAYBILL_HDR
    WHERE  P_WAYBILL_NO = WB_WAYBILL_HDR.WAYBILL_NO
    ;

BEGIN

    OPEN C1;
    FETCH C1
    INTO  CG$DUMMY;
    IF C1%NOTFOUND THEN
      CLOSE C1;
      RAISE NO_DATA_FOUND;
    END IF;
    CLOSE C1;


END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGRI$CHK_WB_WAYBILL_HDR
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGRI$CHK_WB_WAYBILL_HDR */
PROCEDURE CGRI$CHK_WB_WAYBILL_HDR(
   P_CHECK_BOTH IN BOOLEAN       /* Check FKs validated in BOTH (client/server)? */
  ,P_WAYBILL_NO IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Item value                                   */
/* Validate that the deletion of the record is permitted    */
/* by checking for the existence of rows in related tables. */
  CG$DUMMY VARCHAR2(1);  /* Dummy variable */
BEGIN
  /* Deletion of WB_WAYBILL_HDR prevented if WB_WAYBILL_DTL records exist */
  /* Foreign key(s): WDTL_WHDR_FK                                         */
  DECLARE
    CURSOR C IS
      SELECT  '1'
      FROM    WB_WAYBILL_DTL WDTL
      WHERE   WDTL.WAYBILL_NO = P_WAYBILL_NO;
  BEGIN
    OPEN C;
    FETCH C
    INTO    CG$DUMMY;
    IF C%FOUND THEN
      CLOSE C;
      MESSAGE('Error: Cannot delete Waybills while dependent Waybill items exists');
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
    END IF;
    CLOSE C;
  END;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO */
FUNCTION CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO(
   P_SERVER_ERR IN NUMBER        /* Server error message */
  ,P_SERVER_MSG IN VARCHAR2)     /* Server error number  */
RETURN BOOLEAN IS
/* Check and report Primary/Unique Key, Check Constraint and User */
/* Defined Constraint violations                                  */
  constraint_name VARCHAR2(61);  /* Violated constraint */
BEGIN
  /* Check if the error code is one we are interested in */
  IF ( NOT (P_SERVER_ERR IN  (1, 2290) OR
           (P_SERVER_ERR >= 20000 AND P_SERVER_ERR <= 20999) ) )
  THEN
    RETURN( FALSE );
  END IF;

  /* Deal with user defined errors */
  IF (P_SERVER_ERR >= 20000 AND P_SERVER_ERR <= 20999) THEN
    MESSAGE('Error: '||CGTE$STRIP_FIRST_ERROR(P_SERVER_MSG));
    RETURN( TRUE );
  END IF;

  /* Deal with Primary/Unique Key and Check Constraint violations */
  constraint_name := CGTE$STRIP_CONSTRAINT(P_SERVER_MSG);
  IF (P_SERVER_ERR = 1) THEN
    IF (constraint_name = 'WHDR_PK') THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Row exists already with same Waybill No');
    ELSE
      MESSAGE(P_SERVER_MSG);
    END IF;
  ELSIF (P_SERVER_ERR = 2290) THEN
    MESSAGE(P_SERVER_MSG);
  END IF;
  RETURN( TRUE );
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Function
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGTE$WB_WAYBILL_HDR_ERRORS
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGTE$WB_WAYBILL_HDR_ERRORS */
PROCEDURE CGTE$WB_WAYBILL_HDR_ERRORS IS
/* Trap errors returning from the server and report in a user friendly manner */
BEGIN
  DECLARE
    err_code        CONSTANT NUMBER         := ERROR_CODE;
    err_type        CONSTANT VARCHAR2(3)    := ERROR_TYPE;
    server_err               NUMBER         := abs(DBMS_ERROR_CODE);
    server_msg               VARCHAR2(2000) := DBMS_ERROR_TEXT;
    constraint_name          VARCHAR2(61);
  BEGIN
    IF (err_type = 'FRM' AND
        err_code IN (40506, 40508, 40509, 40510) ) THEN

      /* Remove recursive errors from the top of the stack */
      WHILE (server_err = 604) LOOP
        CGTE$POP_ERROR_STACK(server_err, server_msg);
      END LOOP;

      /* Check and report the generic constraint violations */
      IF ( CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO(server_err, server_msg) ) THEN
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;

      /* Check and report the constraint violations specific to this block */
      constraint_name := CGTE$STRIP_CONSTRAINT(server_msg);

      /* FK - Parent key not found */
      IF (server_err = 2291) THEN
        IF (constraint_name = 'WHDR_VOYA_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Voya Id does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'WHDR_VESS_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Vessel Code does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'WHDR_PORT_ORIGIN_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Origin does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'WHDR_PORT_DESTINATION_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Destination does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'WHDR_EMPL_RCVD_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Received By does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'WHDR_EMPL_CHCK_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Checked By does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'WHDR_CUST_SHIPPER_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Shipper does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'WHDR_CUST_CONSIGNEE_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Consignee does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'WHDR_CONT_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Container Code does not exist');
        ELSE
          MESSAGE(server_msg);
        END IF;
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;

      /* FK - Child record found */
      IF (server_err = 2292) THEN
        IF (err_code = 40510) THEN
          IF (constraint_name = 'WDTL_WHDR_FK') THEN
            MESSAGE('Error: Cannot delete Waybills while dependent Waybill items exists');
          ELSE
            MESSAGE(server_msg);
          END IF;
        ELSIF (err_code = 40509) THEN
          MESSAGE(server_msg);
        END IF;
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;
    END IF;

    IF (err_type = 'FRM' AND
        err_code = 40735  AND
        server_err != 0 ) THEN


      /* Remove recursive errors from the top of the stack */
      WHILE (server_err = 604) LOOP
        CGTE$POP_ERROR_STACK(server_err, server_msg);
      END LOOP;

      /* If error not found, issue default message */
      MESSAGE(err_type||'-'||to_char(server_err)||': '||server_msg);
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
    END IF;

    /* If error not found, issue default message */
    MESSAGE(err_type||'-'||to_char(err_code)||': '||ERROR_TEXT);
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;

  END;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGTE$WB_WAYBILL_DTL_ERRORS
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGTE$WB_WAYBILL_DTL_ERRORS */
PROCEDURE CGTE$WB_WAYBILL_DTL_ERRORS IS
/* Trap errors returning from the server and report in a user friendly manner */
BEGIN
  DECLARE
    err_code        CONSTANT NUMBER         := ERROR_CODE;
    err_type        CONSTANT VARCHAR2(3)    := ERROR_TYPE;
    server_err               NUMBER         := abs(DBMS_ERROR_CODE);
    server_msg               VARCHAR2(2000) := DBMS_ERROR_TEXT;
    constraint_name          VARCHAR2(61);
  BEGIN
    IF (err_type = 'FRM' AND
        err_code IN (40506, 40508, 40509, 40510) ) THEN

      /* Remove recursive errors from the top of the stack */
      WHILE (server_err = 604) LOOP
        CGTE$POP_ERROR_STACK(server_err, server_msg);
      END LOOP;

      /* Check and report the generic constraint violations */
      IF ( CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO(server_err, server_msg) ) THEN
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;

      /* Check and report the constraint violations specific to this block */
      constraint_name := CGTE$STRIP_CONSTRAINT(server_msg);

      /* FK - Parent key not found */
      IF (server_err = 2291) THEN
        IF (constraint_name = 'WDTL_WHDR_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Waybill No does not exist');
        ELSE
          MESSAGE(server_msg);
        END IF;
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;

      /* FK - Child record found */
      IF (server_err = 2292) THEN
        IF (err_code = 40510) THEN
          MESSAGE(server_msg);
        ELSIF (err_code = 40509) THEN
          MESSAGE(server_msg);
        END IF;
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;
    END IF;

    IF (err_type = 'FRM' AND
        err_code IN (41105, 41106) ) THEN
      IF (err_code = 41105) THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Query of Waybill items must be in context of Waybills');
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
    ELSIF (err_code = 41106) THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Insert of Waybill items must be in context of Waybills');
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;
    END IF;

    IF (err_type = 'FRM' AND
        err_code = 40735  AND
        server_err != 0 ) THEN


      /* Remove recursive errors from the top of the stack */
      WHILE (server_err = 604) LOOP
        CGTE$POP_ERROR_STACK(server_err, server_msg);
      END LOOP;

      /* If error not found, issue default message */
      MESSAGE(err_type||'-'||to_char(server_err)||': '||server_msg);
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
    END IF;

    /* If error not found, issue default message */
    MESSAGE(err_type||'-'||to_char(err_code)||': '||ERROR_TEXT);
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;

  END;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGLY$DISPLAY_CANVASES
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGLY$DISPLAY_CANVASES */
PROCEDURE CGLY$DISPLAY_CANVASES(
   P_CANVAS_LIST    IN OUT VARCHAR2      /* List of displayed canvases */
  ,P_CURRENT_CANVAS IN     VARCHAR2      /* Current canvas             */
  ,P_BASE_CANVAS    IN     VARCHAR2) IS  /* Base canvas                */
/* Display the current canvas plus any others in the canvas list */
  canvas_list VARCHAR2(255);  /* List of displayed canvases */
  canvas_to_raise VARCHAR2(255);  /* Canvas to raise to the top */
BEGIN
  IF ( P_CURRENT_CANVAS = P_BASE_CANVAS) THEN
    P_CANVAS_LIST := P_CURRENT_CANVAS || ',';
  ELSE
    P_CANVAS_LIST := replace(P_CANVAS_LIST, P_CURRENT_CANVAS || ',');
    IF ( get_view_property(P_BASE_CANVAS, VISIBLE) = 'FALSE') THEN
      canvas_list := P_CANVAS_LIST;
      WHILE (canvas_list IS NOT NULL) LOOP
        canvas_to_raise := substr(canvas_list, 1, instr(canvas_list, ','));
        canvas_list := replace(canvas_list, canvas_to_raise);
        CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS(rtrim(canvas_to_raise, ','), P_BASE_CANVAS);
      END LOOP;
    END IF;
    P_CANVAS_LIST := P_CANVAS_LIST || P_CURRENT_CANVAS || ',';
  END IF;
  CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS(P_CURRENT_CANVAS, P_BASE_CANVAS);
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGLY$GET_RELATED_CANVASES
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGLY$GET_RELATED_CANVASES */
PROCEDURE CGLY$GET_RELATED_CANVASES(
   P_CURRENT_CANVAS IN OUT VARCHAR2      /* Current canvas */
  ,P_BASE_CANVAS    IN OUT VARCHAR2) IS  /* Base canvas    */
/* Find the canvases associated with the current canvas and record which */
/* base canvas is displayed in each window                               */
BEGIN
  IF ( P_CURRENT_CANVAS = 'CG$SPREAD_TABLE_1') THEN
    P_CURRENT_CANVAS := 'CG$PAGE_1';
  END IF;
  /* CFLT */
  P_BASE_CANVAS := P_CURRENT_CANVAS;
  IF (get_view_property(P_CURRENT_CANVAS, WINDOW_NAME) = 'DATE_LOV_WINDOW') THEN
    copy(P_BASE_CANVAS, 'CG$CTRL.CG$WINDOWDATE_LOV_WINDOW_PAGE');
  ELSIF (get_view_property(P_CURRENT_CANVAS, WINDOW_NAME) = 'WINDOW') THEN
    IF (name_in('CG$CTRL.CG$WINDOWWINDOW_PAGE') IS NULL OR name_in('CG$CTRL.CG$WINDOWWINDOW_PAGE') != P_BASE_CANVAS) THEN
      set_view_property('CG$SPREAD_TABLE_1', VISIBLE, PROPERTY_OFF);
    END IF;
    copy(P_BASE_CANVAS, 'CG$CTRL.CG$WINDOWWINDOW_PAGE');
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS */
PROCEDURE CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS(
   P_CANVAS      IN VARCHAR2      /* Current canvas */
  ,P_BASE_CANVAS IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Base canvas    */
/* Raise the current canvas, plus any dependant canvases to the top */
BEGIN
  set_view_property(P_CANVAS, VISIBLE, PROPERTY_ON);
  IF ( P_BASE_CANVAS = 'CG$PAGE_1') THEN
    set_view_property('CG$SPREAD_TABLE_1', VISIBLE, PROPERTY_ON);
    set_view_property('CG$STACKED_HEADER_1', VISIBLE, PROPERTY_ON);
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGLY$CANVAS_MANAGEMENT
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGLY$CANVAS_MANAGEMENT */
PROCEDURE CGLY$CANVAS_MANAGEMENT IS
/* Top level canvas management procedure */
  current_canvas VARCHAR2(61) := get_item_property(name_in('SYSTEM.CURSOR_ITEM'), ITEM_CANVAS);
  base_canvas VARCHAR2(61);
  canvas_list VARCHAR2(255);
BEGIN
  IF ( (name_in('CG$CTRL.CG$LAST_CANVAS') IS NULL) OR (name_in('CG$CTRL.CG$LAST_CANVAS') != current_canvas) ) THEN
    copy(current_canvas, 'CG$CTRL.CG$LAST_CANVAS');
    set_window_property( get_view_property( current_canvas, WINDOW_NAME ), VISIBLE, PROPERTY_ON);
    CGLY$GET_RELATED_CANVASES(current_canvas, base_canvas);
    IF ( base_canvas = 'CG$PAGE_1') THEN
      canvas_list := name_in('CG$CTRL.CG$PAGE_1_LIST');
    END IF;
    CGLY$DISPLAY_CANVASES(canvas_list, current_canvas, base_canvas);
    IF ( base_canvas = 'CG$PAGE_1') THEN
      copy(canvas_list, 'CG$CTRL.CG$PAGE_1_LIST');
    END IF;
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGBS$TOGGLE
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGBS$TOGGLE */
PROCEDURE CGBS$TOGGLE(
   P_QUERY_MODE IN OUT VARCHAR2) IS  /* Query Mode */
/* Toggle query mode between BSMON and BSMOFF, set all query mode items, */
/* display query mode message, set the relations and ensure that the     */
/* canvas is coordinated.                                                */
BEGIN
  /* Toggle the mode */
  IF (P_QUERY_MODE != 'A') THEN
    P_QUERY_MODE := 'A';
  ELSE
    P_QUERY_MODE := 'N';
  END IF;
  /* Set all the items */
  CGBS$SET_QUERY_MODE( P_QUERY_MODE );
  /* Display query mode messages */
  CGBS$MESSAGE_QUERY_MODE( P_QUERY_MODE );
  /* Set the relations */
  CGBS$.SET_RELATIONS( P_QUERY_MODE );
  /* If the query mode is AutoQuery, coordinate outstanding blocks */
  IF (P_QUERY_MODE = 'A') THEN
    CGBS$.COORD_VISIBLE_BLKS( name_in('SYSTEM.CURSOR_BLOCK') );
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGBS$SET_QUERY_MODE
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGBS$SET_QUERY_MODE */
PROCEDURE CGBS$SET_QUERY_MODE(
   P_QUERY_MODE IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Query Mode */
/* Set all query items to the current query mode */
BEGIN
  NULL;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGBS$MESSAGE_QUERY_MODE
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGBS$MESSAGE_QUERY_MODE */
PROCEDURE CGBS$MESSAGE_QUERY_MODE(
   P_QUERY_MODE IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Query Mode */
/* Send a message to the status line indicating the current query mode */
BEGIN
  IF (P_QUERY_MODE = 'A') THEN
    NULL;
  ELSE
    MESSAGE('Auto-query mode off');
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CHECK_VALUATION
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

PROCEDURE check_valuation IS
   nMinR Number(12,2);
begin
   --IF :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_PAYMENT_MODE in ('AO', 'PO') THEN
   --   nMinR := sf_get_lcl_min_rate(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_WAYBILL_DATE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_SHIPPER, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_ORIGIN, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_DESTINATION, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.BASIS);
   --ELSE
   --   nMinR := sf_get_lcl_min_rate(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_WAYBILL_DATE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_CONSIGNEE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_ORIGIN, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_DESTINATION, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.BASIS);
   --END IF;
   --if nvl(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT,0) > 0 and
   --   nMinR > :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT 
   --then
	 --	  :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT := nMinR;
   --end if;
   IF :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT = 0 and :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.DECLARED_VALUE > 0 THEN
      IF :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_PAYMENT_MODE = 'AD' then
         :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT := sf_get_valuation(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_WAYBILL_DATE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_CONSIGNEE_VALUATION, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.DECLARED_VALUE);
      ELSIF :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_PAYMENT_MODE = 'AO' then
         :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT := sf_get_valuation(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_WAYBILL_DATE, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_SHIPPER_VALUATION, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.DECLARED_VALUE);
      ELSE
         :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT := sf_get_valuation(:WB_WAYBILL_DTL.WAHD_WAYBILL_DATE, -1, :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.DECLARED_VALUE);
      END IF;
	   :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.TOTAL_AMT := :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.AMT + :WB_WAYBILL_DTL.VALUATION_AMT;   
   END IF;
END;
